## Codex <sup>5/13/2026, 4:41:20 PM</sup>

I’ll trace the frontend header injection and the backend CORS/socket setup first, then patch the smallest place that explains the whole cascade. The repeating failures all point at preflight rejecting `ngrok-skip-browser-warning`, plus Socket.IO CORS being configured differently from Express.

I found the global frontend override in [frontend/src/main.jsx] adding `ngrok-skip-browser-warning` to every request. That turns simple GETs into preflighted CORS requests, so unless the backend explicitly allows that header, the browser blocks everything before your API code runs.

```
import axios from 'axios'

// Configure Axios globally to bypass Ngrok's anti-abuse warning
axios.defaults.headers.common['ngrok-skip-browser-warning'] = 'true';

// Global fetch interceptor to bypass Ngrok's anti-abuse warning screen for all API requests
const originalFetch = window.fetch;
window.fetch = async (...args) => {
  let [resource, config] = args;
  if (typeof resource === 'string' && resource.includes('ngrok-free.dev')) {
    config = config || {};
    config.headers = {
      ...config.headers,
      'ngrok-skip-browser-warning': 'true' // Bypasses the blue "Visit Site" screen
    };
  }
  return originalFetch(resource, config);
};
```

I’m going to make two changes: allow the ngrok header on the backend CORS preflight, and make the WhatsApp socket prefer direct WebSocket so ngrok does not serve its warning page to Socket.IO polling. I’ll also tighten the frontend global header hook so it only targets your configured backend/ngrok URL.

Fixed the CORS/ngrok cascade.

Changed:
- [backend/server.ts](/c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/backend/server.ts:25): added explicit CORS origins and allowed `ngrok-skip-browser-warning` for Express and Socket.IO.
- [frontend/src/main.jsx](/c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/main.jsx:7): scoped the ngrok header injection to backend/ngrok requests instead of every Axios request globally.
- [frontend/src/components/WhatsAppLogin.jsx](/c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/components/WhatsAppLogin.jsx:7): fixed fallback backend port to `3001` and made Socket.IO WebSocket-only.
- [frontend/src/pages/LiveChat.jsx](/c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/pages/LiveChat.jsx:15): made Socket.IO WebSocket-only to avoid polling CORS failures through ngrok.

Verification:
- `npm run build` in `frontend` passes.
- `npx tsc --noEmit` in `backend` still fails on existing repo TypeScript issues unrelated to this patch.

Restart the backend so the new CORS config is active, then hard-refresh the frontend. The `Request header field ngrok-skip-browser-warning is not allowed` and Socket.IO polling CORS errors should stop.

## Codex <sup>5/13/2026, 4:45:42 PM</sup>

The CORS layer is behaving now; this one is a real backend `401`. I’m going to trace how `Authorization` is built in `Templates` and `Broadcast`, then line it up with the auth middleware so expired tokens get refreshed before those requests fire.

I found two causes. `apiCall` retries after refresh but still reads the old `session` value from React state, and `Broadcast` bypasses `apiCall` entirely, so it never retries on a 401. I’m going to centralize those requests through the refreshed-token helper.

Before editing, I’m keeping this narrow: no backend auth relaxation, just making the frontend send a valid current Supabase token for the calls that already require auth. The server is right to reject expired tokens.

I’m also adding a proactive refresh check so we don’t deliberately send a known-expired token and then rely on a noisy 401 retry. That should reduce the console spam instead of merely recovering from it.

<details>
<summary>Tool: <code>apply_patch</code></summary>

```json
{
  "input": "*** Begin Patch\n*** Update File: frontend/src/context/AuthContext.jsx\n@@\n         // Utility function for API calls with automatic token refresh\n         apiCall: async (url, options = {}) => {\n             const makeRequest = async (retryCount = 0, tokenOverride = null) => {\n                 try {\n-                    const { data: { session: currentSession } } = await supabase.auth.getSession()\n+                    let { data: { session: currentSession } } = await supabase.auth.getSession()\n+                    const expiresAtMs = currentSession?.expires_at ? currentSession.expires_at * 1000 : null\n+                    const isExpiring = expiresAtMs && expiresAtMs < Date.now() + 60_000\n+\n+                    if (!tokenOverride && isExpiring) {\n+                        console.log('Token expired or expiring soon, refreshing before request...')\n+                        const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.refreshSession()\n+                        if (error) throw error\n+                        currentSession = data.session\n+                        if (data.session) {\n+                            setSession(data.session)\n+                            setUser(data.session.user)\n+                        }\n+                    }\n+\n                     const token = tokenOverride || currentSession?.access_token || session?.access_token;\n                     if (!token) throw new Error('No session token');\n*** End Patch\n"
}
```

One catch: the template creation path uploads `FormData`, so the shared helper must not force `Content-Type: application/json` for that request. I’m adjusting that now so the browser can set the multipart boundary correctly.

<details>
<summary>Tool: <code>apply_patch</code></summary>

Fixed the `401` path.

What changed:
- [AuthContext.jsx](/c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/context/AuthContext.jsx:116): `apiCall` now reads the latest Supabase session directly, refreshes tokens proactively when they are expired/about to expire, and retries once with the new token on `401`.
- [Broadcast.jsx](/c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/pages/Broadcast.jsx:61): replaced raw `fetch(... Bearer ${token})` calls with `apiCall`, including template loading.
- [Templates.jsx](/c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/pages/Templates.jsx:47): list/delete/create template requests now all use `apiCall`. Template creation still supports `FormData` correctly.

Verification:
- `npm run build` in `frontend` passes.

Hard-refresh the app after Vite reloads. The `/api/whatsapp/templates` request should now use a fresh token instead of firing with an expired one.

Important WhatsApp detail I found: an image header in a template is not the actual image that gets sent forever. Meta stores it as a sample for approval; when sending that template, you must provide a fresh header image/video/document parameter. If you don’t, Meta can throw `(#132012) Parameter format does not match`. I’ll add UI for that in Broadcast and make the backend send header media parameters correctly.

Done.

Changes:
- Inbox/Shared Inbox box fixed: Live chat now stays locked to the viewport; outer page scroll won’t push it up/down.
- Contacts page buttons working:
  - `Add Contact` opens form and saves contact.
  - `Import CSV` works. CSV columns can be like `name,phone,tags`.
  - Tag filter/reset works.
  - Contact delete button now deletes.
- Template preview:
  - If Meta/API gives an actual media URL, image will show.
  - If not, it now clearly shows that the image header is attached as a Meta approval sample.
- Broadcast `(#132012) Parameter format does not match`:
  - For IMAGE/VIDEO/DOCUMENT header templates, Broadcast now asks for a public header media URL.
  - Backend sends that URL as the required WhatsApp template `header` parameter.

How to send image-header template:
1. Go to `Broadcasting`.
2. Create campaign.
3. Select audience.
4. Select approved template.
5. If template has image header, paste a public image URL in `Header image URL`.
6. Map body variables if any.
7. Launch.

Important: WhatsApp template me jo image approval ke time upload hoti hai, woh sirf sample hoti hai. Actual send karte waqt WhatsApp ko image URL/media parameter dobara chahiye, warna `#132012` aa sakta hai.

Verified: `frontend` build passes. Backend restart karna zaroori hai because contacts APIs and broadcast send logic backend me changed hai.

- Manual URL paste bhi allowed hai, but it must be real `http/https` URL.
- Empty/example URL par next/launch block hoga.
- Backend now gives a clearer failure: missing header media URL.

## My request for Codex:
baar-baar isliye ho raha hai kyunki template send payload mein required image parameter abhi bhi nahi ja raha.

Aapka ads template image header template hai. Isme WhatsApp ko send time par image chahiye.

Fix karo

Broadcast banate waqt HEADER IMAGE URL mein direct image link paste karo, jaise:

https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1460925895917-afdab827c52f

Lekin better hai .jpg direct image URL use karo:

https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1460925895917-afdab827c52f?w=1200

Phir campaign dobara send karo.

Agar phir bhi same error aaye

To problem aapke platform ke backend mein hai. Backend image URL le raha hai, lekin Meta API payload mein add nahi kar raha.

Correct payload mein yeh component hona chahiye:

"components": [
  {
    "type": "header",
    "parameters": [
      {
        "type": "image",
        "image": {
          "link": "YOUR_IMAGE_URL"
        }
      }
    ]
  }
]
Quick Alternative

Meta mein ek new template without image header banao:

Header: blank / none
Body: text only
Button: URL CTA

Phir us template se broadcast bhejo. Usme image URL ki zaroorat nahi padegi.

Final

Issue contacts ka nahi hai. Issue template ka hai: image header required parameter missing.

Fixed the backend side more robustly.

What I changed:
- Backend now accepts header media URL from multiple possible fields:
  - `_header_media_url`
  - `header_media_url`
  - `headerImageUrl`
  - `header_image_url`
- Before saving campaign, backend normalizes it into:
  - `_header_media_type: "image"`
  - `_header_media_url: "https://..."`
- During Meta send, backend now builds the correct payload:

```json
{
  "type": "header",
  "parameters": [
    {
      "type": "image",
      "image": {
        "link": "YOUR_IMAGE_URL"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

Also updated frontend to send both nested and top-level header media fields, so backend definitely receives it.

Verified: frontend build passes.

Important now:
1. Restart backend.
2. Hard refresh frontend.
3. Create a new campaign.
4. Select `ads`.
5. Paste real image URL, for example:
   `https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1460925895917-afdab827c52f?w=1200`
6. Send again.

Old failed campaigns will still show failed. New campaign should include the required image header parameter.

## My request for Codex:
Root Cause Confirmed

Aapke variable_mapping column mein sirf:

{
  "_template_body": "..."
}

save ho raha hai.

Missing keys:

_header_media_type
_header_media_url
header_media_type
header_media_url

Isliye WhatsApp ko required image parameter nahi mil raha, aur error aata hai:

(#131008) Required parameter is missing

Exact Problem

Frontend mein image URL enter karne ke baad bhi handleLaunch() ke payload mein header media fields save nahi ho rahe ya backend insert ke time drop ho rahe hain. Broadcast.jsx mein in keys ko variable_mapping mein add karna intended hai.

What Should Be Saved

Latest campaign ka variable_mapping kuch is tarah dikhna chahiye:

{
  "_template_body": "Hello! Want to generate more leads and sales with Meta Ads?",
  "_header_media_type": "image",
  "_header_media_url": "https://db.getaipilot.in/storage/v1/object/public/wa-media/847e859b-9bd7-4407-93c7-84e6b7a499f2/broadcast-template-headers/1778672820606-2325469c-bf2d-4ee8-8f6c-054f49b25e32.jpg",
  "header_media_type": "image",
  "header_media_url": "https://db.getaipilot.in/storage/v1/object/public/wa-media/847e859b-9bd7-4407-93c7-84e6b7a499f2/broadcast-template-headers/1778672820606-2325469c-bf2d-4ee8-8f6c-054f49b25e32.jpg"
}
Fix in Backend

Jab campaign save ho raha ho (POST /api/broadcast/send), ensure this code runs before insert:

const variableMapping = {
  ...(req.body.variable_mapping || {})
};

if (req.body.header_media_url) {
  variableMapping._header_media_type = req.body.header_media_type || 'image';
  variableMapping._header_media_url = req.body.header_media_url;
  variableMapping.header_media_type = req.body.header_media_type || 'image';
  variableMapping.header_media_url = req.body.header_media_url;
}

Aur insert mein:

variable_mapping: variableMapping
Quick Test

Fix ke baad naya campaign run karein, phir SQL:

select name, variable_mapping
from public.w_campaigns
order by created_at desc
limit 1;

Agar _header_media_url dikh jaye, issue solve ho gaya.

Final Diagnosis

✅ Image URL valid hai
✅ Template approved hai
❌ header_media_url database mein save nahi ho raha

Actual fix: backend mein header_media_url aur header_media_type ko variable_mapping JSONB ke andar persist karna. 🚀

```js
const variableMapping = {
  ...(req.body.variable_mapping || {})
};

if (req.body.header_media_url) {
  variableMapping._header_media_type = req.body.header_media_type || 'image';
  variableMapping._header_media_url = req.body.header_media_url;
  variableMapping.header_media_type = req.body.header_media_type || 'image';
  variableMapping.header_media_url = req.body.header_media_url;
}
```

I found the source of the spam: both socket clients were created at module load with `websocket` only, so they start reconnecting immediately and never fall back if ngrok rejects WS. I’m switching them to connect only when the component mounts, allow polling fallback, and cap retries.

Fixed the socket spam.

What changed:
- Socket no longer auto-connects when the file imports.
- It connects only when `LiveChat` or `WhatsAppLogin` mounts.
- It now tries `websocket` first, then falls back to `polling`.
- Reconnect attempts are capped at 5, so console won’t spam endlessly.
- Socket disconnects cleanly when the page/component unmounts.

Files:
- [LiveChat.jsx](/c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/pages/LiveChat.jsx:15)
- [WhatsAppLogin.jsx](/c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/components/WhatsAppLogin.jsx:10)

Verified: frontend build passes.

After Vite reload/hard refresh, those repeated `WebSocket connection ... failed` lines should stop. If ngrok WebSocket still fails, Socket.IO will use polling fallback instead of hammering the console.

I see one more deterministic gap: backend needs a frontend-provided `required_header_type`, because Meta template lookup can fail to identify the header even though the selected template is image-header. I’m adding that field and making backend reject/persist from it before campaign insert.

Good catch. Your SQL confirmed the actual bug: latest row still had only `_template_body`, so the campaign was being inserted without header media keys.

I added a stronger deterministic fix:

- Frontend now sends `required_header_type: "image"` along with:
  - `header_media_type`
  - `header_media_url`
  - nested `variable_mapping._header_media_url`
- Backend now uses `required_header_type` before DB insert.
- If image URL is missing, backend rejects the campaign before saving.
- If image URL is present, backend forcibly writes all four keys into `variable_mapping`:

```json
{
  "_header_media_type": "image",
  "_header_media_url": "...",
  "header_media_type": "image",
  "header_media_url": "..."
}
```

Also normalized `selectedHeaderFormat` to uppercase in frontend so `IMAGE/image` casing can’t break detection.

Verified: frontend build passes.

Now do this exact sequence:
1. Restart backend.
2. Hard refresh browser.
3. Create a new campaign.
4. Select `ads`.
5. Paste/upload header image.
6. Send.
7. Run SQL again.

If backend is actually restarted on the same ngrok target, latest `variable_mapping` should finally include `_header_media_url`.

Fixed the backend side in [server.ts](</c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/backend/server.ts:4849>).

What changed:
- After campaign insert, backend now force-updates `variable_mapping` again with the header image fields.
- `processCampaign()` now protects against a stale/incomplete DB row and uses the launch payload mapping if DB refetch is missing header media.
- Added Meta failure logs showing the exact template `components` being sent, so if Meta still says `#131008`, we’ll know the missing parameter precisely.

Important: restart your backend server/ngrok process, then create a new campaign. Old failed campaigns will not change.

After sending, run:

```sql
select name, template_name, variable_mapping, results
from public.w_campaigns
order by created_at desc
limit 1;
```

Now `variable_mapping` should include:

```json
"_header_media_type": "image",
"_header_media_url": "...jpg",
"header_media_type": "image",
"header_media_url": "...jpg"
```

Ab missing parameter solve ho gaya, isliye error change hua: `#131005 Access denied`. That usually means Meta accepted the structure, but kisi value par permission/access issue aa raha hai. Your mapping shows button URL me full `https://metabulluniverse.com/` diya gaya hai; URL button templates often sirf placeholder suffix maangte hain, full URL nahi. function parseVars(components) {
```
    const body = components?.find(c => c.type === 'BODY')?.text || ''
    return [...new Set((body.match(/\{\{(\d+)\}\}/g) || []).map(m => m.replace(/\D/g, '')))]
}

function parseDynamicUrlButtons(components) {
    const buttons = components?.find(c => c.type === 'BUTTONS')?.buttons || []
    return buttons
        .map((button, index) => ({
            index,
            text: button.text || `Button ${index + 1}`,
            url: button.url || ''
        }))
        .filter(button => String(button.url).includes('{{'))
}
```

```
        .filter(button => String(button.url).includes('{{'))

function normalizeDynamicUrlButtonValue(button, value) {
    let cleanValue = String(value || '').trim()
    const templateUrl = String(button?.url || '')
    const placeholderIndex = templateUrl.indexOf('{{')
    const staticPrefix = placeholderIndex >= 0 ? templateUrl.slice(0, placeholderIndex) : ''

    if (staticPrefix && cleanValue.startsWith(staticPrefix)) {
        cleanValue = cleanValue.slice(staticPrefix.length)
    }

    if (staticPrefix.endsWith('/') && cleanValue.startsWith('/')) {
        cleanValue = cleanValue.slice(1)
    }

    return cleanValue
}
```

```
        source.headerImageUrl ||
        source.header_image_url ||
        source.headerUrl ||
        ''
    ).trim();

    return { type, url };
}

function normalizeDynamicUrlButtonValue(templateUrl: string, value: any) {
    let cleanValue = String(value || '').trim();
    const cleanTemplateUrl = String(templateUrl || '');
    const placeholderIndex = cleanTemplateUrl.indexOf('{{');
    const staticPrefix = placeholderIndex >= 0 ? cleanTemplateUrl.slice(0, placeholderIndex) : '';

    if (staticPrefix && cleanValue.startsWith(staticPrefix)) {
        cleanValue = cleanValue.slice(staticPrefix.length);
    }

    if (staticPrefix.endsWith('/') && cleanValue.startsWith('/')) {
        cleanValue = cleanValue.slice(1);
    }

    return cleanValue;
}

function formatIndianPhoneForDisplay(value: string | null | undefined): string {
    const key = normalizeIndianPhoneKey(value);
    if (!key) {
        const dig
...(truncated)
```

Ab `#131005 Access denied` ka reason almost certainly URL button domain/prefix mismatch hai.

Tumne `button_url_0` me full different URL diya:

```json
"https://getaipilot.com/pricing"
```

Meta dynamic URL button me usually approved template ke URL ka sirf placeholder part allow hota hai. Agar template approved URL, for example:

```txt
https://metabulluniverse.com/{{1}}
```

to `getaipilot.com/pricing` nahi chalega. Us template ke liye sirf suffix/value chalegi, jaise:

```txt
pricing
```

Maine ab hard fix add kiya:
- UI me approved URL dikhega: `Approved URL: ...`
- Agar tum different full domain paste karoge, app launch se pehle block karega.
- Backend bhi same validation karega, so failed campaign create nahi hoga.
- Agar approved prefix match karta hai, e.g. approved `https://getaipilot.com/{{1}}` and tum paste karo `https://getaipilot.com/pricing`, app automatically `pricing` save karega.

Retest:
1. Backend restart.
2. Frontend hard refresh.
3. Template select karo.
4. `Required URL button value` ke neeche jo `Approved URL` dikhega usko dekho.
5. Usme `{{1}}` ki jagah sirf value daalo, full different domain nahi.

Frontend build pass hai. Backend `tsc` still old unrelated errors dikha raha hai.

```
// GET /api/broadcast/tags
app.get('/api/broadcast/tags', authMiddleware, async (req, res) => {
    const orgId = (req as any).organization_id;
    try {
        const { data: contacts, error: fetchErr } = await supabase
            .from('w_contacts')
            .select('tags')
            .eq('organization_id', orgId);
            
        if (fetchErr) throw fetchErr;
        
        const tagsSet = new Set<string>();
        contacts?.forEach((c: any) => {
            if (Array.isArray(c.tags)) {
                c.tags.forEach((t: string) => tagsSet.add(t));
            }
        });
        
        res.json({ tags: Array.from(tagsSet) });
    } catch (err: any) {
        console.error('Fetch Tags Error:', err);

    }
});
```

```
                else text = field || ''; 
                
                renderedText = renderedText.replace(`{{${num}}}`, text);
                parameters.push({ type: 'text', text: text || ' ' });
            }

                components.push({ type: 'body', parameters });

                to: recipient,

                }
```

Ab payload issue nahi hai. Meta log clear bol raha hai:

`There was a problem with the access token or permissions`

Maine backend me fix add kiya:
- [server.ts](</c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/backend/server.ts:127>) token permissions inspect karega using Meta `debug_token`.
- Manual account save karte waqt token missing `whatsapp_business_messaging` hua to save block hoga.
- Broadcast launch se pehle token missing permissions hua to campaign create nahi hoga.
- Agar Meta phir bhi `#131005` de, history me ab clear error save hoga: token/phone-number permission mismatch.

Ab actual action:
1. Backend restart karo.
2. Connect Account page par Meta account reconnect/save karo.
3. Token must have:
   - `whatsapp_business_messaging`
   - `whatsapp_business_management`
4. Same token ke WABA ke andar selected `phone_number_id` hona chahiye.

Iske bina code se message send nahi hoga, kyunki Meta API permission deny kar rahi hai. Header image, button URL, variable mapping ab correct ja rahe hain.

```
// Delete account
app.delete('/api/whatsapp/accounts/:id', authMiddleware, async (req, res) => {
    const { id } = req.params;
    const orgId = (req as any).organization_id;
    try {
        const { error } = await supabase
            .from('w_wa_accounts')
            .update({ status: 'disconnected', access_token_encrypted: null })

            .eq('organization_id', orgId); // Ensure user can only delete their own accounts
```

Yeh error ab code/template ka nahi hai. Payload correct ja raha hai:

- header image component present
- URL button component present
- `button_url_0: "contact-us"` correct placeholder value hai

Meta ab bol raha hai:

`(#131005) Access denied`
`problem with the access token or permissions`

Meaning: selected WhatsApp account ka token is `phone_number_id` se message send karne ke liye authorized nahi hai.

Maine ab app me diagnostic add kar diya:

- Backend: [server.ts](</c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/backend/server.ts:165>) account/token diagnostics
- Endpoint: `/api/whatsapp/accounts/:id/diagnostics`
- Frontend: [WhatsAppConnect.jsx](</c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/pages/WhatsAppConnect.jsx:246>) each Meta account card me `Check Send Access` button

Ab karo:
1. Backend restart karo.
2. Frontend hard refresh.
3. `Connect Account` page open karo.
4. Meta API account card par `Check Send Access` click karo.
5. Jo issue dikhega, uske according reconnect karo.

Most likely fix:
- Meta Business Settings me System User token banao.
- Token permissions:
  - `whatsapp_business_messaging`
  - `whatsapp_business_management`
- Same WABA/phone number ko us System User ko assign karo.
- Phir Connect Account page me wahi WABA ID + token save karo.

Frontend build pass hai. Backend `tsc` still old unrelated TypeScript errors dikha raha hai.

## Codex <sup>5/13/2026, 6:35:44 PM</sup>

Nice, this is working now.

The broadcast shows `4 sent / 0 failed`, and WhatsApp received the template with:
- header image
- body text
- footer
- URL CTA button

So the real chain was:

1. Missing header image parameter
2. Then missing URL button parameter
3. Then wrong token/account permissions
4. Now fixed after using a send-capable Meta token/account

Current result is correct.
